  <div class="markdown-body f5 mb-2">
    <p>Natural language processing (NLP) is a field of computer science that studies how computers and humans interact. In the 1950s, Alan Turing published an article that proposed a measure of intelligence, now called the Turing test. More modern techniques, such as deep learning, have produced results in the fields of language modeling, parsing, and natural-language tasks.</p>

                  <p>Many models have identical implementations of <code>prune_heads</code> it would be nice to store that implementation as a method on <code>PretrainedModel</code> and reduce the redundancy.</p>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>I was going though the existing enhancement issues again and though it'd be nice to collect ideas for spaCy plugins and related projects. There are always people in the community who are looking for new things to build, so here's some inspiration <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="sparkles" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2728.png">✨</g-emoji>  For existing plugins and projects, check out the <a href="https://spacy.io/universe" rel="nofollow">spaCy universe</a>.</p>
<p>If you have questions about the projects I suggested,</p>

<p>Here's a detailed explanation including screenshots</p>
<p><a href="https://help.botpress.io/t/how-to-redirect-to-an-external-url-while-using-a-button-made-in-choice-skill/1791" rel="nofollow">https://help.botpress.io/t/how-to-redirect-to-an-external-url-while-using-a-button-made-in-choice-skill/1791</a></p>
<p>This option will be really beneficial  using choice skill buttons since at the moment, you can only add an ext</p>

              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  mahdiman
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2018-12-27T20:02:12Z" class="no-wrap">Dec 27, 2018</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>As per the StanfordCoreNLP <a href="https://nlp.stanford.edu/nlp/javadoc/javanlp/edu/stanford/nlp/ling/CoreLabel.html" rel="nofollow">documentation for CoreLabel</a>, The functions <strong>after()</strong> and <strong>before()</strong> should return white space strings between the token and the next/previous tokens respectively.<br>
However, they return an empty string always even if there are some white spaces when the tokenizer option **normalizeOth</p>

                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"

            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  ychong
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2018-02-08T03:35:47Z" class="no-wrap">Feb 7, 2018</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Hi I would like to propose a better implementation for 'test_indices':</p>
<p>We can remove the unneeded np.array casting:</p>
<p>Cleaner/New:<br>
test_indices = list(set(range(len(texts))) - set(train_indices))</p>
<p>Old:<br>
test_indices = np.array(list(set(range(len(texts))) - set(train_indices)))</p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
                    style="background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255,255,255,1), rgba(255,255,255,0));"
                  >

                      Read more
</a>                  </div>
